Geonames codes

This page is an auxiliary page used for development of g5.
It lists C1 (administrative code level 1) and C2 (administrative code level 2) codes for the countries present in the database.
This list is generated by 
php run-g5.php db look geo
  • AT Austria
  • BE Belgium
  • CH Switzerland
  • CL Chile
  • CZ Czech Republic
